		#specifics for plane types must be put before general ones which will be added anyway, hence my goal in the long run to have only unit type specfic icon selections.

		#Future note for anyone else who might be fiddling in this document: In the list of icons, the game will use the GFX that is last inside the icons pool as the default for that specific plane type.
		#So if you have GFX_light_plane_4_medium below GFX_GER_early_fighter_medium for Interwar Planes for Germany, all German Interwar plane designs will default to GFX_light_plane_4_medium.
		#The artwork also shows up in order in the drop down menu, meaning that if you want, you can sort out the list from more historical looks by having them further down the list. 

		#Remember; The list has a priority system that is Lowest to Highest. Meaning the higher up on the list, the lower priority for the game.
